Let me talk about my experience of staying here for five days and four nights:

1. The room is spacious, the bed is super easy to sleep on, and the toilet in the bathroom is a flush toilet.
2. There are free late-night snacks every night from 22:00 to 23:30, including pig heart soup, preserved egg and lean meat porridge, seafood noodles, white fungus sweet soup... delicious.
3. There is a lake behind the hotel. After a meal or getting up in the morning, you can go for a walk on the lakeside trail.
4. The hotel provides free airport pick-up and drop-off.
5. Free hot and cold drinks are provided in the hotel lobby.
6. Unlimited supply of bottled water (placed in front of the elevator entrance).
7. On Mother‚Äôs Day, I received snacks and flowers from the hotel, as well as a small blessing card.
8. The hotel‚Äôs butler Ruan Jianpeng is very considerate. If we ask any questions, he will reply immediately. He will also remind us of the midnight snack time and midnight snack map every day.

name:T‚ÄçO‚ÄçL‚ÄçI‚ÄçY‚ÄçA
info:Superior Double Room
info:Stayed in July 2023
info:Family
info:12 Reviews
rating:4.7
posted:Posted July 18, 2023
msg:It is a hotel worth recommending. The bed in the room is very comfortable, and the environment is also very good. The reception in the lobby on the first floor is also very different (aviation level). The hotel waiters are a beautiful sight. The gym, the infinity h swimming pool, and the sauna all brought me a very pleasant experience. It is a pity that you will not feel bored even if you spend a day in the hotel. The hotel provides a free supper (after 22 o'clock), I went to taste it, it tastes good, but eating it so late is not good for your health, it would be better if you can replace it with breakfast :)

I only gave four points for sanitation, because there are blood stains from previous guests on the side of the toilet and hair in the bathroom and room. Five-star hotels should clean up more carefully
In addition, the sound insulation of the door is a bit poor. At 6 o'clock in the morning, I often hear the sound of the guests next door knocking on the door and talking in other rooms.

Generally speaking, this is a hotel that makes our whole family very satisfied, and it will definitely be this hotel next time in Xiamen.
